< review>
I like it because it's local but it's expensive compared to other beauty supplies and they don't allow returns or exchanges..

I don't like doing business anywhere I can't return or at least exchange an item... I bought hair for braiding that I ended up not being able to use because my braider said it would cut her fingers....It was never opened and I had the receipt and they wouldn't let me bring it back so I'm stuck with five packs of hair that I can never use...

If it was a wig or something I could see, but something in a package that has clearly never been opened you should at least be able to exchange!

This is a policy that is typical of a lot of Asian Merchants which is why I don't do swap meets and don't really like to patronize them because it's not the American way...

So due to their no exchange policy, I will not be shopping there again..<//review>

< review>
I've been searching for a wig store around my house for a while now and decided just go in here on a whim. Man, I'm so glad I did!! They have so many different types of wigs available-and they allow you to try them on (with the purchase of a $1 wig cap) which is awesome since not many places let you do that. I went in looking for something very specific-a yellow lace front wig and I mean a bright yellow. Instead of just telling me no they didn't have that, they actually took the time to look for some wigs that were similar. Despite not being a bright yellow, they ended up showing me one that I really loved so I went ahead and purchased it! They have this stamp card too that once you purchase 4 lace wigs, your 5th one is 40% off which is pretty cool-and I know I'll use it since I'm always buying wigs! I was really nervous going in here that the service wasn't going to be that great or that they wouldn't have anything I liked, but I was very impressed with this store. The customer service was amazing and their selection of products was huge! Besides just wigs, they also carry a ton of different beauty supplies like hair care products, make up and others things. Definitely my new favorite beauty supply store. I highly recommend it!<//review>

<Text>This 9 hole disc golf course is an Oasis surrounded by industry and city. Power lines, radio towers and several cell phone towers mark the perimeter of the course, which is a large bowl of grass and some trees.

While the park has trees, Culver City Oil Fields is the dominant view in the distance. And a pocket of West LA and Downtown LA.

Some decently long holes.  Holes 2-4 are heavily pock-marked by ground rodents and has large areas of holey dirt and mowed dead grasses.

There are a few beautiful Huge oak trees, and the course is clean and well maintained. 9 holes are fairly easy to find.

It's not pretty, nor is it challenging, and the course is exposed to wind and the entire park is pretty busy around sunset.

The throwers are rushed, like the people in this city. There are picnics and wanderers inside the course area, to watch for if you have any wild guns throwing in your party.

The high rating is due to lack of other course options in the Los Angeles area, not the creative challenge of this course.

The Good:  It's a real 9 hole course and it's in the West LA area. Good for beginners/intermediate.< /Text><user_id>114896264612751979681</user_id><user_name>Boulder Studios< /user_name><Rating>2<//Rating>< Pics>
None</Pics>

<rate>5</rate>< text>
Big fan of this course. 9 holes going back and forth across the top of the park. All par 3 from about 200 ft to 350 in length. Some good elevation shots. There can be some pedestrians who do not understand disc golf but overall pretty open. Parking costs money but playing is free. Usually not too crowded. Have only had to wait a couple times to tee off. Concrete tee pads, not the best signage to point your way but its hard to get super lost. Would recommend.</text>

< Review>
Greg just finished the semi-annual service of our heating & air conditioning system (we replaced the original equipment that was installed in 2003 with new Day & Night equipment).

I let him know that our A/C unit has been very noisy lately and he assured me the compressor was fine and said the noise was from housing vibrating-he installed isolation pads and is running less noisily. However, since we had very little space at the side of our home, he said the more vertical Day & Night fans tend to be noisier since they spin vertically and not the more common horizontal position.

He then moved on to checking the air handler, heater and filter condition (all located in the upper floor/attic. He said everything was functioning great and was done with the service.

I appreciated his willingness to discuss the A/C noise problem and some air balancing issues we have between the floors/rooms. He also was responsive when I asked him to put on "booties" when going to the upper floor.

All-in-all, a pleasant chap and another reason why I continue to be a 1 Hour customer!

Tim Craig< /Review>

<Rate>5</Rate><text>March 31, 2021 update:  No annual A/C maintenance visit in 2020 due to COVID-19 issues, which is understandable.  But on March 6 I sent an e-mail to Bigham's, requesting their lost experienced tech for my upcoming 2021 visit, since the 2019 check found a full pound low on R-410A refrigerant.  So I was worried that my now 6-year old system might have a refrigerant leak.  The good news is no leak found, refrigerant charge was still full.  Bigham's tech concluded that when system was installed in 2015 a small leak in the outdoor compressor's Schrader valve was missed.  Since that valve also has a cover cap with its own gasket, it took 4 years for enough refrigerant to finally leak out to cause an undercharge condition, meaning that my central AC was working a lot harder than it should have.  Valve leak was apparently fixed during the 2019 visit, as part of the refrigerant adding process, so 2021 visit found still full refrigerant charge and proper operation.  Kudos to Bigham's for sending one of their most experienced techs, Mr. William Sage with 26 years of HVAC experience, and for his thorough check and explanation.  I continue to be a satisfied Bigham's customer and a Home Protection Club member; the membership cost for having annual checks of my central AC, furnace, and electrical, is well worth it.

Sept 18, 2019:  Bigham's One-Hour Heating and Air Conditioning installed a new central air and furnace system in 2015, and did a great job.  In September 2019, during the annual central air Home Protection Club (HPC) visit, I mentioned that my central air seemed to be struggling to keep my house cool.  The Bigham's tech found that I was a full pound low on R-410A refrigerant; installing more refrigerant lowered the plenum temperature by a full 10 degrees, and now my central air has no problem keeping my house cool.

The bad news was that the Bigham's tech advised that he would have to charge me $378 for the refrigerant.  What?  Almost $400 for just one pound of refrigerant?  On a four-year old system?  But, I authorized the charge.

I then followed up with Bigham's One-Hour Heating and Air Conditioning;  Why wasn't this handled as a warranty repair, at no additional cost?  My central air came with a 10-year warranty, after all.

Bigham's reviewed my query, and advised that this should have been a no-additional-charge warranty repair.  A refund will be processed.

So, kudos again to Bigham's One-Hour Heating and Air Conditioning.  They rectified the problem.  Well done to Kathleen (Kat) Gillett and Chris Gentry of Bigham's.  This is one reason why Bigham's is Diamond Certified.<//text>< Pics>
